----------------------------------- SOURCE BEGIN -------------------------------------
import java.util.*;

public class NumberFreq {
	static Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		int t = input.nextInt();
		int[] lst = new int[2000];
		int[] count = new int[2000];
		freq(t, lst, count);
	}

	private static void freq(int t, int[] lst, int[] count) {
		int[] n = new int[t];
		for (int i = 0; i < t; ++i) {
			n[i] = input.nextInt();
			for (int j = 0; j < lst.length; ++j) {
				if (n[i] == j) {
					++count[j];
				}
			}
		}
		Arrays.sort(int[] n);
		for (int i < 0; i<n.length; ++i) {
			System.out.printf("%d aparece %d vez(es)\n", , count[]);
		}
	}
}

----------------------------------- SOURCE END -------------------------------------

import java.util.*;

public class NumberFreq {
	static Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		int t = input.nextInt();
		int[] lst = new int[2000];
		int[] count = new int[2000];
		freq(t, lst, count);
	}

	private static void freq(int t, int[] lst, int[] count) {
		int[] n = new int[t];
		for (int i = 0; i < t; ++i) {
			n[i] = input.nextInt();
			for (int j = 0; j < lst.length; ++j) {
				if (n[i] == j) {
					++count[j];
				}
			}
		}
		Arrays.sort(int[] n);
		for (int i < 0; i<n.length; ++i) {
			System.out.printf("%d aparece %d vez(es)\n", , count[n[]1]);
		}
	}
}

import java.util.*;

public class NumberFreq {
	static Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		int t = input.nextInt();
		int[] lst = new int[2000];
		int[] count = new int[2000];
		freq(t, lst, count);
	}

	private static void freq(int t, int[] lst, int[] count) {
		int[] n = new int[t];
		for (int i = 0; i < t; ++i) {
			n[i] = input.nextInt();
			for (int j = 0; j < lst.length; ++j) {
				if (n[i] == j) {
					++count[j];
				}
			}
		}
		Arrays.sort(int[] n);
		for (int i < 0; i<n.length; ++i) {
			System.out.printf("%d aparece %d vez(es)\n", , count[n[]);
		}
	}
}

----------------------------------- SOURCE BEGIN -------------------------------------
import java.util.*;

public class NumberFreq {
	static Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		int t = input.nextInt();
		int[] lst = new int[2000];
		int[] count = new int[2000];
		freq(t, lst, count);
	}

	private static void freq(int t, int[] lst, int[] count) {
		int[] n = new int[t];
		for (int i = 0; i < t; ++i) {
			n[i] = input.nextInt();
			for (int j = 0; j < lst.length; ++j) {
				if (n[i] == j) {
					++count[j];
				}
			}
		}
		Arrays.sort(int[] n);
		for (int i < 0; i<n.length; ++i) {
			System.out.printf("%d aparece %d vez(es)\n", , count[n[i]]);
		}
	}
}

----------------------------------- SOURCE END -------------------------------------

----------------------------------- SOURCE BEGIN -------------------------------------
import java.util.*;

public class NumberFreq {
	static Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		int t = input.nextInt();
		int[] lst = new int[2000];
		int[] count = new int[2000];
		freq(t, lst, count);
	}

	private static void freq(int t, int[] lst, int[] count) {
		int[] n = new int[t];
		for (int i = 0; i < t; ++i) {
			n[i] = input.nextInt();
			for (int j = 0; j < lst.length; ++j) {
				if (n[i] == j) {
					++count[j];
				}
			}
		}
		Arrays.sort(int[] n);
		for (int i < 0; i<n.length; ++i) {
			System.out.printf("%d aparece %d vez(es)\n", n, count[n[i]]);
		}
	}
}

----------------------------------- SOURCE BEGIN -------------------------------------
import java.util.*;

public class NumberFreq {
	static Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		int t = input.nextInt();
		int[] lst = new int[2000];
		int[] count = new int[2000];
		freq(t, lst, count);
	}

	private static void freq(int t, int[] lst, int[] count) {
		int[] n = new int[t];
		for (int i = 0; i < t; ++i) {
			n[i] = input.nextInt();
			for (int j = 0; j < lst.length; ++j) {
				if (n[i] == j) {
					++count[j];
				}
			}
		}
		Arrays.sort(int[] n);
		for (int i < 0; i<n.length; ++i) {
			System.out.printf("%d aparece %d vez(es)\n", n[]i, count[n[i]]);
		}
	}
}

----------------------------------- SOURCE END -------------------------------------

----------------------------------- SOURCE BEGIN -------------------------------------
import java.util.*;

public class NumberFreq {
	static Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		int t = input.nextInt();
		int[] lst = new int[2000];
		int[] count = new int[2000];
		freq(t, lst, count);
	}

	private static void freq(int t, int[] lst, int[] count) {
		int[] n = new int[t];
		for (int i = 0; i < t; ++i) {
			n[i] = input.nextInt();
			for (int j = 0; j < lst.length; ++j) {
				if (n[i] == j) {
					++count[j];
				}
			}
		}
		Arrays.sort(int[] n);
		for (int i < 0; i<n.length; ++i) {
			System.out.printf("%d aparece %d vez(es)\n", n[, count[n[i]]);
		}
	}
}

----------------------------------- SOURCE END -------------------------------------

----------------------------------- SOURCE BEGIN -------------------------------------
import java.util.*;

public class NumberFreq {
	static Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		int t = input.nextInt();
		int[] lst = new int[2000];
		int[] count = new int[2000];
		freq(t, lst, count);
	}

	private static void freq(int t, int[] lst, int[] count) {
		int[] n = new int[t];
		for (int i = 0; i < t; ++i) {
			n[i] = input.nextInt();
			for (int j = 0; j < lst.length; ++j) {
				if (n[i] == j) {
					++count[j];
				}
			}
		}
		Arrays.sort(int[] n);
		for (int i < 0; i<n.length; ++i) {
			System.out.printf("%d aparece %d vez(es)\n", n[i], count[n[i]]);
		}
	}
}

----------------------------------- SOURCE BEGIN -------------------------------------
import java.util.*;

public class NumberFreq {
	static Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		int t = input.nextInt();
		int[] lst = new int[2000];
		int[] count = new int[2000];
		freq(t, lst, count);
	}

	private static void freq(int t, int[] lst, int[] count) {
		int[] n = new int[t];
		for (int i = 0; i < t; ++i) {
			n[i] = input.nextInt();
			for (int j = 0; j < lst.length; ++j) {
				if (n[i] == j) {
					++count[j];
				}
			}
		}
		Arrays.sort(int[] n);
		for (int i < 0; i<n.length; ++i) {
			System.out.printf("%d aparece %d vez(es)\n", n[i], count[n[i]]);
		}
	}
}

----------------------------------- SOURCE BEGIN -------------------------------------
import java.util.*;

public class NumberFreq {
	static Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		int t = input.nextInt();
		int[] lst = new int[2000];
		int[] count = new int[2000];
		freq(t, lst, count);
	}

	private static void freq(int t, int[] lst, int[] count) {
		int[] n = new int[t];
		for (int i = 0; i < t; ++i) {
			n[i] = input.nextInt();
			for (int j = 0; j < lst.length; ++j) {
				if (n[i] == j) {
					++count[j];
				}
			}
		}
		Arrays.sort(int[] n);
		for (int i = 0; i<n.length; ++i) {
			System.out.printf("%d aparece %d vez(es)\n", n[i], count[n[i]]);
		}
	}
}

----------------------------------- SOURCE BEGIN -------------------------------------
import java.util.*;

public class NumberFreq {
	static Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);

	public static void main(String[] args) {
		int t = input.nextInt();
		int[] lst = new int[2000];
		int[] count = new int[2000];
		freq(t, lst, count);
	}

	private static void freq(int t, int[] lst, int[] count) {
		int[] n = new int[t];
		for (int i = 0; i < t; ++i) {
			n[i] = input.nextInt();
			for (int j = 0; j < lst.length; ++j) {
				if (n[i] == j) {
					++count[j];
				}
			}
		}
		Arrays.sort(int[] n);
		for (int i = 0; i<n.length; ++i) {
			System.out.printf("%d aparece %d vez(es)\n", n[i], count[n[i]]);
		}
	}
}
